/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[DACfnGetBeginSchoolYear]    Script Date: 9/10/2018 10:06:42 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO




-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Li, Joyce>
-- Create date: <7/30/2008>
-- Description:	<This function returns the BeginSchoolYear value with the VotingStartDate
--               that's passed in as a parameter.>
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[DACfnGetBeginSchoolYear]
(
	@paramDate DATETIME
)
RETURNS INT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ResultVar INT

  IF DATEPART(month, @paramDate) >= 8
    BEGIN
      SET @ResultVar = DATEPART(year, @paramDate)
    END
  ELSE
    BEGIN
      SET @ResultVar = DATEPART(year, @paramDate) - 1
    END
	
  RETURN @ResultVar

END





GO

(HISD network time). 
<br>
<B>DAC Voting Procedures for Campus-Based Teachers and other Campus-Based Professionals:</B>
Following submission of all of the nominees, a district ballot will be opened for electronic voting via a secured HISD portal application. At the conclusion of the voting window, nominees with the most votes will be notified of their election to the DAC.<br><br>

Each campus-based professional is eligible to cast one (1) teacher vote and one (1) other professional vote.<br><br>

Individual teachers at elementary schools will elect one person from among the elementary teacher nominees.<br><br>

Individual teachers at middle schools and PK-8 campuses will elect one person from among the middle school and PK-8 campus nominees.<br><br>

Individual teachers at high schools and 6-12 campuses will elect one person from among the high school nominees.<br><br>

Individual campus and district professional personnel (non-teachers) may elect one person from among the other professional nominees.<br><br>

<b>DAC Voting Procedures for Central Office-Based Professionals:</b>
Central office professionals, <b>paygrade 25</b> and above, are eligible to cast one (1) vote and may elect one person from the central office nominees.<br>

<br>

To vote for the nominees, click on Cast Your Vote link on this page. Once you click on the button "Vote", a message will appear saying "Is this your final vote?"   Once "OK" is clicked, your ballot is cast and it cannot be changed. Voting results will be made available to the public on <B><ResultsAvailableStartDatePlaceHolder></B>. <br><br>

If you need additional information about DAC election procedures, please contact Bernadette Cardenas or Jesse Marche at 713-556-7022. For technical questions, please contact the HISD Service Desk.<br> 
Thank you for your participation.<br> <br>

Office of School Support<br>
